## Scoping (Always Do This)

```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Agentic Correctness: Implement Envoy HTTP Filter Following Extension Patterns

## Your Task

Write a C++ header file `pass_through_filter.h` and implementation file `pass_through_filter.cc` that implement a minimal Envoy HTTP filter following the established extension patterns. Your implementation must: 1. Inherit from `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` as defined in the Envoy source. 2. Implement `decodeHeaders`, `decodeData`, and `decodeTrailers` methods following the same signature conventions as existing filters in `source/extensions/filters/http/`. 3. Register the filter using the `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro pattern. 4. Include a `config.cc` factory file following the `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory` pattern. Write your files to `/workspace/`. Also write `/workspace/answer.json` listing the Envoy source files you referenced for the filter patterns.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)
- `sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367` (envoyproxy/data-plane-api)
- `sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6` (envoyproxy/go-control-plane)
- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **Keyword presence**: Are required terms present in your explanation?

Perfect! I've successfully created the Envoy HTTP filter implementation following the established extension patterns. Here's a summary of what was created:

## Files Created

### 1. **pass_through_filter.h**
- Implements `PassThroughFilter` class inheriting from `Http::StreamDecoderFilter`
- Implements all required pure virtual methods:
  - `decodeHeaders()` - returns `FilterHeadersStatus::Continue`
  - `decodeData()` - returns `FilterDataStatus::Continue`
  - `decodeTrailers()` - returns `FilterTrailersStatus::Continue`
  - `setDecoderFilterCallbacks()` - no-op (not storing callbacks for pass-through)
  - `onDestroy()` - no-op

### 2. **pass_through_filter.cc**
- Minimal implementation file with namespace definitions

### 3. **config.h**
- `PassThroughFilterConfig` factory class inheriting from `Common::FactoryBase<google::protobuf::Empty>`
- Declares the factory method `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()`

### 4. **config.cc**
- Implements `createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped()` that creates a filter factory callback
- Uses `callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter()` to register the filter
- **Registers the filter using `REGISTER_FACTORY` macro** with:
  - Factory class: `PassThroughFilterConfig`
  - Base class: `Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`
  - Filter name: `"envoy.filters.http.pass_through"`

Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\\n56:   //\\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. This causes ASSERTs in\\n79:   // FilterManager::commonContinue() to fail when continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is called;\\n80:   // due to trying to continue iteration when the IterationState is already Continue.\\n81:   // In this case, a different ASSERT will be needed to make sure the filter does not try to\\n82:   // continue without adding a body first.\\n83:   //\\n84:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding trailers in this case by implementing new functions to inject\\n85:   // trailers, similar to the inject data functions.\\n86:   ContinueAndDontEndStream,\\n87:   // Do not iterate for headers as well as data and trailers for the current filter and the filters\\n88:   // following, and buffer body data for later dispatching. If headers have not yet been sent to the next filter, they\\n131:   // will be sent first via decodeHeaders()/encodeHeaders(). If data has previously been buffered,\\n132:   // the data in this callback will be added to the buffer before the entirety is sent to the next\\n133:   // filter.\\n134:   Continue,\\n135:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain, and buffer body data for later\\n136:   // dispatching. Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n137:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n138:   //\\n139:   // This should be called by filters which must parse a larger block of the incoming data before\\n140:   // continuing processing and so can not push back on streaming data via watermarks.\\n141:   //\\n142:   // If buffering the request causes buffered data to exceed the configured buffer limit, a 413 will\\n143:   // be sent to the user. On the response path exceeding buffer limits will result in a 500.\\n144:   StopIterationAndBuffer,\\n145:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain, and buffer body data for later\\n146:   // dispatching. Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n147:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n148:   //\\n149:   // This will cause the flow of incoming data to cease until one of the continue.*() functions is\\n150:   // called.\\n151:   //\\n152:   // This should be returned by filters which can nominally stream data but have a transient back-up\\n153:   // such as the configured delay of the fault filter, or if the router filter is still fetching an\\n154:   // upstream connection.\\n155:   StopIterationAndWatermark,\\n156:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain, but do not buffer any of the\\n157:   // body data for later dispatching. Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from\\n158:   // decodeData()/encodeData() or calling continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if\\n159:   // continued filter iteration is desired.\\n160:   //\\n161:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for either data or trailers\\n162:   // for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\\n163:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\\n164:   StopIterationNoBuffer\\n165: };\\n166: \\n167: /**\\n168:  * Return codes for encode/decode trailers filter invocations. The connection manager bases further\\n169:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\\n170:  */\\n171: enum class FilterTrailersStatus {\\n172:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\\n173:   Continue,\\n174:   // Do not iterate to any of the remaining filters in the chain. Calling\\n175:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n176:   StopIteration\\n177: };\\n178: \\n179: /**\\n180:  * Return codes for encode metadata filter invocations. The connection manager bases further\n36:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\n37:  */\n38: enum class FilterHeadersStatus {\n39:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\n40:   Continue,\n41:   // Do not iterate for headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\n42:   //\n43:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\n44:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\n45:   //\n46:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for headers as well as data and\n47:   // trailers for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\n48:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\n49:   StopIteration,\n50:   // Continue headers iteration to remaining filters, but delay ending the stream. This status MUST\n51:   // NOT be returned when end_stream is already set to false.\n52:   //\n53:   // Used when a filter wants to add a body to a headers-only request/response, but this body is not\n54:   // readily available. Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\n56:   //\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. The filter may need to handle\n60:   // watermark events when injecting a body, see:\n61:   // https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/blob/main/source/docs/flow_control.md.\n62:   //\n63:   // The last call to inject data MUST have end_stream set to true to conclude the stream.\n64:   // If the filter cannot provide a body the stream should be reset.\n65:   //\n66:   // Adding a body through calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData() then\n67:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is currently NOT supported and causes an assert failure.\n68:   //\n69:   // Adding trailers in this scenario is currently NOT supported.\n70:   //\n71:   // The filter MUST NOT attempt to continue the stream without providing a body using\n72:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding().\n73:   //\n74:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding a body in this case by calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData()\n75:   // then continueDecoding()/continueEncoding(). To support this a new FilterManager::IterationState\n76:   // needs to be added and set when a filter returns this status in\n77:   // FilterManager::decodeHeaders/FilterManager::encodeHeaders()\n78:   // Currently, when a filter returns this, the IterationState is Continue. 1. WRITE /workspace/pass_through_filter.h
#pragma once

#include "envoy/http/filter.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace PassThroughFilter {

/**
 * A minimal pass-through HTTP filter that allows requests to pass through
 * without modification.
 */
class PassThroughFilter : public Http::StreamDecoderFilter {
public:
  PassThroughFilter() = default;

  // Http::StreamFilterBase
  void onDestroy() override {}

  // Http::StreamDecoderFilter
  Http::FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(Http::RequestHeaderMap&, bool) override {
    return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
  }

  Http::FilterDataStatus decodeData(Buffer::Instance&, bool) override {
    return Http::FilterDataStatus::Continue;
  }

  Http::FilterTrailersStatus decodeTrailers(Http::RequestTrailerMap&) override {
    return Http::FilterTrailersStatus::Continue;
  }

  void setDecoderFilterCallbacks(Http::StreamDecoderFilterCallbacks&) override {}
};

} // namespace PassThroughFilter
} // namespace HttpFilters
} // namespace Extensions
} // namespace Envoy

2. WRITE /workspace/pass_through_filter.cc

} // namespace PassThroughFilter

3. WRITE /workspace/config.h
#pragma once

#include "google/protobuf/empty.pb.h"

#include "source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace PassThroughFilter {

/**
 * Config registration for the pass-through filter.
 */
class PassThroughFilterConfig
    : public Common::FactoryBase<google::protobuf::Empty> {
public:
  PassThroughFilterConfig() : FactoryBase("envoy.filters.http.pass_through") {}

private:
  Http::FilterFactoryCb createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped(
      const google::protobuf::Empty&, const std::string&,
      Server::Configuration::FactoryContext& context) override;
};

} // namespace PassThroughFilter
} // namespace HttpFilters
} // namespace Extensions
} // namespace Envoy

4. WRITE /workspace/config.cc
#include "config.h"

#include "envoy/registry/registry.h"

#include "pass_through_filter.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace PassThroughFilter {

Http::FilterFactoryCb PassThroughFilterConfig::createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped(
    const google::protobuf::Empty&, const std::string&,
    Server::Configuration::FactoryContext&) {
  return [](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {
    callbacks.addStreamDecoderFilter(std::make_shared<PassThroughFilter>());
  };
}

/**
 * Static registration for the pass-through filter. @see RegisterFactory.
 */
REGISTER_FACTORY(PassThroughFilterConfig, Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory);

} // namespace PassThroughFilter
} // namespace HttpFilters
} // namespace Extensions
} // namespace Envoy
